td-js-loaded\" itemscope=\"itemscope\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/WebPage\"><div class=\"bt_gistbutton_hidden_content\" style=\"display:none;\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-257987\" src=\"http://images.newsworldindia.in/2017/04/saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800.jpg\" alt=\"saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800\" width=\"700\" height=\"525\">\n\nTwo FIRs were today registered against BJP's Lok Sabha member Raghav Lakhanpal , 12 persons, in connection with two incidents of violence in Saharanpur, police said.\n\nSSP Love Kumar said a First Information Report (FIR) was registered against over 300 people in connection with the stone-pelting by members of two communities yesterday during a rally to mark Ambedkar Jayanti at Sadak Dudhali village.\n\n<strong>ALSO READ:&nbsp;<a href=\"http://newsworldindia.in/india/stone-pelting-in-up-injures-several-including-mp-and-senior-police-officer/257758/\">Stone Pelting In UP Injures Several, Including MP And Senior Police Officer</a></strong>\n\nThe charges include IPC section 148 (rioting, armed with deadly weapon), 332 (voluntarily causing hurt to deter public servant from his duty), 336 (endangering life or personal safety of others) among others.\n\nThe second FIR has been registered in connection with theprotest outside the Senior Superintendent of Police's residence in which a CCTV camera was damaged and his\"nameplate removed\", he said, adding the FIR was registered with charges similar to the first one.\n\nThe SSP further said in both the FIRs it has been mentioned that local MP Raghav Lakhanpal Sharma was present at both the spots.\n\nNo arrest has been made in this connection so far, the SSP said.\n\nAt present, the situation is under control in the area while heavy police force has been deployed to prevent any untoward incident.\n\nThe rally yesterday taken out to mark BR Ambedkar's birth anniversary in Sadak Dudhali village was allegedly objected to by members of a community who started pelting stones.\n\nMP Raghav Lakhanpal Sharma and SSP Kumar were among several people who suffered injuries in the ensuing stone pelting from both the sides. Some other policemen were also injured.\n\nFollowing this, police reached the spot and pacified boththe groups. However, the MP along with his supporters reached outside the SSP's official residence and started protesting demanding conduct of the rally and suspension of the Senior Superintendent of Police.\n\nThey damaged a CCTV camera outside the SSP's residenc eafter which police personnel from nearby areas were deployed there.\n\nThe SSP had said permission for the rally was not given by the administration.\n\nA flag march was yesterday carried out in the village.\n\n&nbsp;</div>    \n\t\n    <script type=\"text/javascript\">\n    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {\n        //AddhiddenData\n        $(\"body\").append(\"<input type='hidden' id='titleForGistButton' value='Saharanpur Violence: 2 FIR&#8217;s Registered Against BJP&#8217;s Lok Sabha Member Raghav Lakhanpal' />\");\n        $(\"body\").append(\"<input type='hidden' id='pubIdForGistButton' value='66dce0b5863f436350fe05545ae48bd6' />\");\n        $(\"body\").append(\"<input type='hidden' id='ImgForGistButton' value='https://images.newsworldindia.in/2017/04/saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800.jpg' />\");\n       \n    });\n    </script>\n        <script type=\"text/javascript\" src=\"https://www.gistai.com/widget/gistbutton_wp.js\"></script> \n    <script type=\"text/javascript\"> gistButton.options({publisher: \"66dce0b5863f436350fe05545ae48bd6\", autoload: false, sharable: true, option: 1});</script>\n    \n    \n\t\t<script type=\"text/javascript\">\n\n\t\t\tjQuery(document).ready(function() {\n\n\t\t\t\t// CUSTOM AJAX CONTENT LOADING FUNCTION\n\n\t\t\t\tvar ajaxRevslider = function(obj) {\n\n\t\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// obj.type : Post Type\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// obj.id : ID of Content to Load\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// obj.aspectratio : The Aspect Ratio of the Container / Media\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// obj.selector : The Container Selector where the Content of Ajax will be injected. class=\"socialBuzzLine\"><div class=\"sbL\"><div class=\"socialBuzzLine\"><div class=\"sbSocial sbSocialData\" data-title=\"Saharanpur Violence: 2 FIR’s Registered Against BJP’s Lok Sabha Member Raghav Lakhanpal\" data-via=\"NWI\" data-perma=\"https://newsworldindia.in/india/saharanpur-violence-2-firs-registered-against-bjps-lok-sabha-member-raghav-lakhanpal/257986/\"><!-- following can \">+</div></div></div></div><div class=\"sbClr\"></div></div><script type=\"text/javascript\">var sbFBAPPID = '100008193301178';</script><!--/SB--><p><img class=\"lazy-hidden aligncenter size-full wp-image-257987 td-animation-stack-type0-1\" src=\"data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7\" data-lazy-type=\"image\" data-src=\"http://images.newsworldindia.in/2017/04/saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800.jpg\" alt=\"saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800\" width=\"700\" height=\"525\"><noscript>&lt;img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-257987\" src=\"http://images.newsworldindia.in/2017/04/saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800.jpg\" alt=\"saharanpur-violence_647_042217085800\" width=\"700\" height=\"525\" /&gt;</noscript></p>\n<p>Two FIRs were today registered against BJP’s Lok Sabha member Raghav Lakhanpal , 12 persons, in connection with two incidents of violence in Saharanpur, police said.</p>\n<p>SSP Love Kumar said a First Information Report (FIR) was registered against over 300 people in connection with the stone-pelting by members of two communities yesterday during a rally to mark Ambedkar Jayanti at Sadak Dudhali village.</p>\n<p><strong>ALSO READ:&nbsp;<a href=\"http://newsworldindia.in/india/stone-pelting-in-up-injures-several-including-mp-and-senior-police-officer/257758/\">Stone Pelting In UP Injures Several, Including MP And Senior Police Officer</a></strong></p>\n<p>The charges include IPC section 148 (rioting, armed with deadly weapon), 332 (voluntarily causing hurt to deter public servant from his duty), 336 (endangering life or personal safety of others) among others.</p>\n<p>The second FIR has been registered in connection with theprotest outside the Senior Superintendent of Police’s residence in which a CCTV camera was damaged and his”nameplate removed”, he said, adding the FIR was registered with charges similar to the first one.</p>\n<p>The SSP further said in both the FIRs it has been mentioned that local MP Raghav Lakhanpal Sharma was present at both the spots.</p>\n<p>No arrest has been made in this connection so far, the SSP said.</p>\n<p>At present, the situation is under control in the area while heavy police force has been deployed to prevent any untoward incident.</p>\n<p>The rally yesterday taken out to mark BR Ambedkar’s birth anniversary in Sadak Dudhali village was allegedly objected to by members of a community who started pelting stones.</p>\n<p>MP Raghav Lakhanpal Sharma and SSP Kumar were among several people who suffered injuries in the ensuing stone pelting from both the sides. Some other policemen were also injured.</p>\n<p>Following this, police reached the spot and pacified boththe groups. However, the MP along with his supporters reached outside the SSP’s official residence and started protesting demanding conduct of the rally and suspension of the Senior Superintendent of Police.</p>\n<p>They damaged a CCTV camera outside the SSP’s residenc eafter which police personnel from nearby areas were deployed there.</p>\n<p>The SSP had said permission for the rally was not given by the administration.</p>\n<p>A flag march was yesterday carried out in the village.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n\n <!-- A generated by theme --> \n\n<script async=\"\"
